# Saltmarrow Strand Microcontent Pack — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part3_2025-12-24_MicroPOIs

600 micro-POIs designed to increase moment-to-moment density.

### Saltmarrow Micro-POI 001: Mire-Skein Tidepool
- **Vibe:** too quiet for the time of day
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Warden's Stew (ID 49017) — Curio Figurine.
- **Node:** Gutterborn Tally (ID 48858) — Material Cloth.
- **Node:** Saltglass Boots (ID 49680) — Material Pigment.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Tide Reavers (dash, knockback)
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Mark the safe route with chalk symbols.
  - Find who keeps ringing the chimes at midnight.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Saltmarrow Micro-POI 002: Rime-Needle Sink
- **Vibe:** too quiet for the time of day
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Glimmerdeep Vial (ID 46845) — Consumable Tea.
- **Node:** Amberwake Helm (ID 48227) — Curio Figurine.
- **Node:** Iron-banded Tea (ID 45855) — Alchemy Item Catalyst.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Stonejaw Boars (charge, stun)
  - Dock Rats (bleed, swarm)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Light three lanterns without being seen.
  - Hunt the pack-leader and return a token.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

  - Lantern Wraiths (fear, light-sensitive)
  - Bogleeches (slow, stacking debuff)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Follow the cant marks to a hidden cache.
  - Bring back a sample for an alchemist’s field kit.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).
